#ALBANIAN SUBJECTS
lezhe_league_member = {
    copy_from = default

    sprite = GFX_icon_albanian_league_of_lezhe_member
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_lead_league_of_lezhe
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_league_of_lezhe

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 20.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 1
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = lezhe_league_member_subject
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = lezhe_league_member_overlord
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_lezhe_league_member
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_lezhe_league_member
}

#ANGEVIN SUBJECTS
anglois_lordship = {
    copy_from = default

    sprite = GFX_icon_anglois_lordship
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_lead_anglois_aristocracy
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_anglois_aristocracy

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.25
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 35.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 1
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
        same_overlord = anglois_lordship
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = anglois_lordship
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = anglois_lordship
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = anglois_lordship
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = lordship_subject
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = lordship_overlord
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_lordship
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_lordship
}

anglois_marquisate = {
    copy_from = march

    # Graphics:
    sprite = GFX_icon_anglois_marquisate #Was GFX_icon_core_eyalet
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_lead_anglois_aristocracy #Was GFX_icon_diplomacy_lead_core_eyalet
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_anglois_aristocracy #Was GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_core_eyalet

    # Properties:
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.15
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 25.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 0.25
    can_be_annexed = yes
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes
    is_march = yes

    # Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = no
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    # Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_marquisate #Was cb_disloyal_eyalet

    # Subject Interactions:

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear # Use this to clear after copy_from.

    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = marquisate_bonus
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = same_religion_subject_bonus_mod
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = same_religion_subject_bonus
                religion = PREV
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = marquisate_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_marquisate
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_marquisate
}

anglois_principality = {
    copy_from = anglois_duchy

    can_be_annexed = no

    request_extra_levies = yes

    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = no
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    # Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_kingdom #Was cb_disloyal_eyalet

    # Subject Interactions:

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear # Use this to clear after copy_from.

    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = kingdom_bonus
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = same_religion_subject_bonus_mod
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = same_religion_subject_bonus
                religion = PREV
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = kingdom_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_kingdom
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_kingdom

    overlord_can_attack = no
    has_power_projection = no

    can_have_subjects_of_other_types = yes
    can_union_break = no
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    transfer_subjects_when_made = yes
    can_concentrate_development = no
    extend_trading_range = yes
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    liberty_desire_negative_prestige = 1.0
    military_focus = 0.66

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    restoration_cb = cb_restore_personal_union

    # Subject Interactions:
    placate_rulers = no
    enforce_culture = yes
    siphon_income = yes
    support_loyalists = yes

    # Modifiers:

        modifier = aragonese_crown_pu_bonus
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        trigger = {
            overlord = { has_government_attribute = personal_union_war_contribution }
        }
        modifier = aragonese_crown_pu_bonus
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            overlord = { has_government_attribute = personal_union_war_contribution }
        }
        modifier = aragonese_crown_pu_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = in_union
    subject_opinion_modifier = in_union
}

    can_rival = {

    }

        same_overlord = austrian_lordship
    }
    can_marry = {

    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no

    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

            overlord = { has_government_attribute = personal_union_war_contribution }
        }
        modifier = austrian_crown_pu_bonus
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            overlord = { has_government_attribute = personal_union_war_contribution }
        }
        modifier = austrian_crown_pu_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = in_union
    subject_opinion_modifier = in_union
}

    copy_from = default

    sprite = GFX_icon_baltic_lordship
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_lead_baltic_aristocracy
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_baltic_aristocracy

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.25
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 35.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 1
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
        same_overlord = baltic_lordship
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = baltic_lordship
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = baltic_lordship
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = baltic_lordship
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = lordship_subject
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = lordship_overlord
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_lordship
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_lordship
}

    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes

    military_focus = 1.2

    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = belgian_barony
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = belgian_barony
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = belgian_barony
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no

    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes

    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes

    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no

    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes

    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto

    }
    modifier_subject = {

            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }

    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_castilian_aristocracy #Was GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_core_eyalet

    # Properties:
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.1
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 20.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 0.25
    can_be_integrated = yes #Changed from can_be_annexed = yes - SF & Prussia
    can_be_annexed = no
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes


    # Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = yes
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = no
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    # Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_principality #Was cb_disloyal_eyalet

    # Subject Interactions:

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear # Use this to clear after copy_from.

    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = principality_bonus #Was castilian_duque_bonus - Edited by Prussia
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = same_religion_subject_bonus_mod
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = same_religion_subject_bonus
                religion = PREV
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = principality_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_principality
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_principality
}

    can_union_break = no
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    transfer_subjects_when_made = yes
    can_concentrate_development = no
    extend_trading_range = yes
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    liberty_desire_negative_prestige = 1.0
    military_focus = 0.66

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    restoration_cb = cb_restore_personal_union

    # Subject Interactions:
    placate_rulers = no
    enforce_culture = yes
    siphon_income = yes
    support_loyalists = yes

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = english_crown_pu_bonus
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        trigger = {
            overlord = { has_government_attribute = personal_union_war_contribution }
        }
        modifier = english_crown_pu_bonus
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                tag = ENG
                tag = GBR
                tag = UNK
            }
            overlord = { has_country_flag = ned_man_o_wars_from_pu_flag }
        }
        modifier = ned_man_o_war_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            overlord = { has_government_attribute = personal_union_war_contribution }
        }
        modifier = english_crown_pu_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = in_union
    subject_opinion_modifier = in_union
}

    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_lead_french_aristocracy
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_icon_diplomacy_am_french_aristocracy

    # Properties:
    has_power_projection = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = no
    separatists_become_subjects = yes
    allows_taking_land_without_independence = yes
    forms_trade_companies = no
    can_concentrate_development = no
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.25
    trust_on_start = 0
    base_liberty_desire = 35.0
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.00
    military_focus = 1.2
    pays_overlord = 1
    joins_overlords_wars = yes
    can_use_claims = yes

    relative_power_class = 1
    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
        same_overlord = french_lordship
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = french_lordship
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = french_lordship
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = french_lordship
    }

    #Subject Interactions
    seize_court_resources = no
    request_extra_levies = yes
    grant_administrative_autonomy = yes
    #(disable)
    scutage = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    grant_province = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    enforce_culture = no
    seize_territory = no
    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    #Modifiers
    modifier_overlord = clear #We don't want to duplicate the ones inherited from vassal
    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = lordship_subject
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_tax_modifier
        trigger = {
            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = lordship_overlord
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_lordship
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_lordship
}

    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_ampuppet

        is_subject = no
        is_nomad = no
        is_tribal = no
        primitives = no
        legitimacy_equivalent = 50
        total_development = 300
    }

    # Properties:
    can_be_annexed = yes
    has_power_projection = no
    can_transfer_in_peace = no
    extend_trading_range = yes

    max_government_rank = 6
    cities_required_for_bonuses = 0 #0
    trust_on_start = 35

    base_liberty_desire = -15.0
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.2
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.2
    military_focus = 1.0

    relative_power_class = 2
    diplomacy_view_class = 1

    can_rival = {
        other_overlord = satellite_state
    }

    # Subject Interactions:
    # (continuous)
    support_loyalists = yes
    subsidize_armies = yes
    # (immediate)
    placate_rulers = yes
    replace_governor = yes
    fortify_march = yes
    seize_territory = yes
    send_additional_troops = yes

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = subject_nation
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = satellite_state_modifier
        trigger = {
            NOT = { development_of_overlord_fraction = 0.33 }
        }
        expiration_message_overlord = MARCHTOOLARGE
        expiration_message_subject = MARCHTOOLARGEUS
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = satellite_state_overlord_has_parliament_modifier
        trigger = {
            FROM = {
                government = monarchy
                has_parliament = yes
            }
        }
    }

    modifier_overlord = clear
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = satellite_state_overlord_modifier
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = vassal_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_satellite_state
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_satellite_state
}

    can_release_in_peace = yes

    can_set_mil_focus = yes

    liberty_desire_revolution = 35.0

    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.15

    relative_power_class = 2

        same_overlord = silesian_duke
        same_overlord = vassal
    }
    can_rival = {
        same_overlord = silesian_duke
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = silesian_duke
        same_overlord = vassal
        same_overlord = march
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = silesian_duke
        same_overlord = vassal
        same_overlord = march
    }

    restoration_cb = cb_disloyal_vassal

    # Subject Interactions:
    scutage = yes
    place_relative_on_throne = yes
    seize_territory = yes
    enforce_religion = yes
    grant_core_claim = yes
    placate_rulers = yes
    enforce_culture = yes
    siphon_income = yes
    takeondebt = yes
    knowledge_sharing = yes

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = silesian_duke_modifier
    }

    modifier_subject = { # Actually penalities vassal recieves for being too large since silesian duchies were rather small and fractured
        trigger = {
            num_of_cities = 5
        }
        modifier = silesian_duke_size_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            num_of_cities = 7
        }
        modifier = silesian_duke_size_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            num_of_cities = 10
        }
        modifier = silesian_duke_size_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            num_of_cities = 14
        }
        modifier = silesian_duke_size_modifier
    }

    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = vassal_subject
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_vassal
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_vassal
}

    enforce_culture = no

    #(enable)
    contribute_to_capital = yes
    return_land = yes
    conscript_general = yes

    modifier_subject = clear #Ditto

            overlord = {
                has_government_attribute = subject_tax_modifier_25
            }
        }
    }

        modifier = earldom_overlord

#MERCHANTLIST REPUBLIC
merchantlist_republic = {
    copy_from = default

    # Graphics:
    sprite = GFX_icon_merchantlist_republic
    diplomacy_overlord_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_merchantlist_republic_leadvassal
    diplomacy_subject_sprite = GFX_diplomacy_merchantlist_republic_amvassal

    # Triggers:
    is_potential_overlord = {
        is_subject = no
        OR = {
            AND = {
                culture_group = latin
                has_government_attribute = is_merchant_republic
            }
            # Custom Rule
            has_government_attribute = can_create_merchantlist_republic_rule
        }
    }

    # Properties:
    transfer_trade_power = yes
    takes_diplo_slot = no
    has_power_projection = no
    gets_help_with_rebels = yes
    extend_trading_range = yes
    can_be_annexed = no

    max_government_rank = 6
    cities_required_for_bonuses = 0
    trust_on_start = 35

    base_liberty_desire = -10
    liberty_desire_development_ratio = 0.15
    liberty_desire_same_dynasty = -5.0
    liberty_desire_revolution = 0
    pays_overlord = 0.25
    forcelimit_to_overlord = 0.05

    relative_power_class = 6
    diplomacy_view_class = 1

    should_quit_wars_on_activation = yes

    can_fight = {
    }
    can_rival = {
    }
    can_ally = {
        same_overlord = merchantlist_republic
    }
    can_marry = {
        same_overlord = vassal
        same_overlord = feudal_republic
        same_overlord = merchantlist_republic
        same_overlord = venetian_republic
        same_overlord = genoese_commercial_republic
    }

    # Subject Interactions:
    # (continuous)
    scutage = yes
    # (immediate)
    seize_territory = yes
    contribute_to_capital = yes

    # Modifiers:
    modifier_subject = clear
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_nation
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = MERCHANTLIST_REPUBLIC_IS_MERCHANT_REPUBLIC_TT
                has_government_attribute = is_merchant_republic
            }
        }
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_merchant_republic_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        trigger = {
            capital_scope = {
                custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                    tooltip = MERCHANTLIST_REPUBLIC_HOME_NODE_HAS_MERCHANT_FROM_OVERLORD_TT
                    has_merchant = FROM
                }
            }
        }
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_overlord_trading_modifier
    }
    modifier_subject = {
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_seized_merchant_fleets_modifier
        trigger = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = MERCHANTLIST_REPUBLIC_HAS_SEIZE_MERCHANT_FLEETS_TT
                has_country_flag = merchantlist_republic_seize_merchant_fleets
            }
        }
    }

    modifier_overlord = clear
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_overlord_modifier
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        trigger = {
            capital_scope = {
                OR = {
                    trade_share = {
                        country = ROOT
                        share = 50
                    }
                    custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                        tooltip = MERCHANTLIST_REPUBLIC_HOME_NODE_OVERLORD_HAS_75_TRADE_POWER_TT
                        trade_share = {
                            country = FROM
                            share = 75
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_merchant_overlord_modifier
    }
    modifier_overlord = {
        modifier = merchantlist_republic_seized_merchant_fleets_overlord_modifier
        trigger = {
            custom_trigger_tooltip = {
                tooltip = MERCHANTLIST_REPUBLIC_HAS_SEIZE_MERCHANT_FLEETS_TT
                has_country_flag = merchantlist_republic_seize_merchant_fleets
            }
            NOT = { liberty_desire = 50 }
        }
    }

    overlord_opinion_modifier = is_merchantlist_republic
    subject_opinion_modifier = is_merchantlist_republic
}

                has_government_attribute = is_merchant_republic
            }
            # Custom Rule
            has_government_attribute = can_impose_genoese_commercial_republic_rules
        }
    }

    # Properties:
